## Opcodes

```
  0: 0x003D [0x1A] CALL_SUBROUTINE(address=0x1491)
  1: 0x0040 [0x03] Work_Zone[2] = ExtData[1]->WorkLocal[1]
  2: 0x0045 [0x00] END_REQSTACK()

  3: 0x1491 [0x41] GET_BIT_WORK_RANGE(start_bit=0*, end_bit=3*, source=Work_Zone[9], result=ExtData[1]->WorkLocal[1])
  4: 0x149A [0x1B] RETURN
```
